      * Dati passati  :  LAREA1                                      *

           EXEC SQL
              DECLARE  CURCATG CURSOR    WITH HOLD FOR
              SELECT
                     H_REGIONE1,
                     H_REGIONE2,
                     H_REGIONE3,
                     H_REGIONE4,
                     H_REGIONE5,
                     H_CODCTG,
                     H_REGCTG,
                     H_ANNOCTG,
                     H_DESCTG,
                     H_PROGCTG,
                     H_FINANZ,
                     H_CONTO1
             FROM  TDSSX00
             WHERE
                   H_REGCTG  >= :H-REGCTG AND
                   H_ANNOCTG >= :H-ANNOCTG
           END-EXEC.

      *                                                              *
      *-------------------------------------------------------------*
      *       Tabella per call a RDSPD06 per dettaglio recuperi     *
      *-------------------------------------------------------------*
       01  LTABRECUPERI.
           10  LRECELEM  occurs 30 times.
               15  LRECCOREAL    pic  X(003)   value spaces.
               15  LRECCORENU    pic  9(005)   value 0.
               15  LRECIMUREE    pic  9(5)V99  value 0.
      *-------------------------------------------------------------*
      *       CAMPI PER CALL PGM STAMPA B.C. 730                    *
      *-------------------------------------------------------------*
      *-----------------Definizioni necessarie alle routine usate    *
      *-------------------------------------------------------------*
      *-----    AREA PER CHIAMATA AL CONGUAGLIO 730        --------*
      *-------------------------------------------------------------*
      *17072020
      *    COPY POPCSIN.
      *
      *-----------------------------------------Per routine 'RNPYEAR'
           copy CNPYEAR.
      *--------------------------------------------- Routine  RDSDLY1*
       01  PER-RDSDLY1.
           02  R-TEMPO                 pic 99.
      *-----------------------------------------per routine "RDSUSR1"*
       01  PER-RDSUSR1.
           02  ID-LAVORO               pic x(10).
           02  RD-LAVORO  redefines  ID-LAVORO.
               04  ID8-LAVORO          pic x(08).
               04  filler              pic x(02).
           02  ID-UTENTE               pic x(10).
      *-----------------------------------------per routine "PDSPD16"*
       01  AREALINK-1.
           03 C-CODICE-SEDE           pic 9(04)  value zeros.
           03 C-NOME-SEDE             pic x(22)  value spaces.
           03 C-CODICE-STOP           pic 9(02)  value zeros.
           03 C-NOME-STOP             pic x(22)  value spaces.
           03 C-PROCEDURA             pic x(03)  value spaces.
           03 C-TIPOCALCOLO           pic x(01)  value spaces.
      *                       = "S"  simulazione x lista contrrollo  *
      *                       = "R"  reale x pagamento prestazione   *
           03 C-RICHIESTA             pic x(01)  value spaces.
      *                    se =  I - lettura Informazioni            *
      *                       =  C - richiesta progressivo Calcolo   *
      *                       =  E - Indica Elaborazione in corso    *
      *                       =  F - Fine elaborazione               *
      *                       =  R - ristampe                        *
           03 C-PROGRESSIVO           pic 9(03)  value zeros.
           03 C-RETCODE               pic x      value spaces.
      *             se  =  E - elaborazione in Errore (non eseguita) *
      *             se  =  C - elaborazione Completata Correttamente *
      *             se  =  D - struttura Disattiva                   *
      *             se  =  N - elaborazione Non eseguita             *
       01  AREALINK-2.
           03 C-DIRIGENTE             pic x(30)  value spaces.
           03 C-ELABINCORSO           pic x      value spaces.
      *              se =  Y - Elaboraz. Yn corso medesima struttura *
      *                 =  K - Elaboraz. Kompletata                  *
           03 C-CONGUAGLIO            pic 9(2)   value zeros.
      *
      *-----------------------------------------Per routine 'PDSPD13'*
       01  PER-PDSPD13.
           03  Z-MATRICOLA            pic s9(08).
           03  Z-RETCODE              pic  x(01).
      *-----------------------------------------Per routine 'RDSTART'*
           copy  CDSTART1.
      *
      *--------------------------------------------------------------*
      *CONSTANT SECTION.
      *77 WK_VERSION     pic s9(9) comp-5  value is 20090915.
      *--------------------------------------------------------------*
       LINKAGE SECTION.
       01  COMMAREADS.
           03  LAREA1.
           05 L-CODICE-SEDE         pic 9(04).
           05 L-NOME-SEDE           pic x(22).
           05 L-CODICE-STOP         pic 9(02).
           05 L-NOME-STOP           pic x(22).
           05 L-PROCEDURA           pic x(03).
           05 L-TIPOCALCOLO         pic x(01).
           05 L-RICHIESTA           pic x(01).
           05 L-PROGRESSIVO         pic 9(03).
           05 L-RETCODE               pic x.
      *    se L-RETCODE =  "N" elaborazione Non effettuata
      *    se           =  "C" elaborazione Completata Correttamente
      *    se           =  "E" elaborazione in Errore
           03  LAREA-D.
           05  LCODOPE                pic x(02).
           05  LLIVAUTO               pic x(01).
           05  LMATRICOLA             pic x(08).
           03  L-DATAELABO            pic 9(08).
           03  FILLER                 PIC X(26922).
      *==============================================================*
       PROCEDURE  DIVISION  using  COMMAREADS.
       MAIN.
           perform  I00-INIZIALI      thru  I00-EX.
           perform  C00-CENTRALI      thru  C00-EX.
           perform  F00-FINALI        thru  F00-EX.
       MAIN-EX. exit.
      *
       A10-AGGIORNA.
      *-------------------------------------------- Elab. x ristampa *
      *
           if  L-RICHIESTA  =  "R"
               go  to  A10-EX
           END-IF.
      *
           move  L-PROCEDURA      to H-PPROCEDURA .
           move  L-CODICE-STOP    to H-PSTRUTTURA .
           move  "N"              to H-PBACKUP    .
      *
           PERFORM A10-DB2-SELECT THRU A10-DB2-SELECT-EX.
           IF SQLCODE NOT = 0
      *        move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
      *        move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
      *        perform  T73-TESTO73    thru  T73-EX
      *        perform  W10-MSGERRORE  thru  W10-EX
                EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT ROLLBACK END-EXEC
               go  to  A10-EX
           ELSE
               if  F-LRIEPILOGO  =   0
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
                   move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
                   EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT ROLLBACK END-EXEC
                   perform  T73-TESTO73    thru  T73-EX
                   perform  W10-MSGERRORE  thru  W10-EX
               end-if
           end-IF.
      *------------------------------------------?? Elab. x ristampa *
      *    if  L-RICHIESTA  =  "R"
      *------------------------------------------?? Elab. x NULLO    *
           if H-PZEROPAGAM   =  "S"    and
gga           H-PCODTELEMA  =  "NULLO"
           then
               EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT ROLLBACK END-EXEC
               go  to  A10-FLAGYNCORSO
           end-if.
      *
           if H-PIMPCONTAB                    =  zeroes
           then
               continue
           else
               if (H-PIMPCONTAB                    >  zeroes)  and
                  (H-PIMPTELEMA                    >  zeroes)  and
                  (H-PIMPCONTAB                    not  equal
                   H-PIMPTELEMA )
               then
                   continue
               else
                   EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT ROLLBACK END-EXEC
                   go  to  A10-FLAGYNCORSO
               end-if
           end-if.
      *
           if  W-ERRORE  =  "N"
           then
               if  W-CENTRA  equal  spaces
               then  continue
               else
                   perform  A20-TELEMATICO  thru  A20-EX
                   if  W-ERRORE  =  "S"
                   then
                       move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
                       EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT ROLLBACK END-EXEC
      *                go  to  A10-EX
                   end-if
               end-if
           end-if.
      *------------------------------- Aggiorno record RIEPILOGO     *
      *    if  F-LRIEPILOGO  =  "00"   and
           if  W-ERRORE  =  "N"
           then
               perform  A12-UPD-RIEPILOGO  thru  A12-EX
           else
               move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
               move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
               EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT ROLLBACK END-EXEC
           end-if.
      *------------------------------------ Memorizzo fine elaboraz. *
       A10-FLAGYNCORSO.
           if  W-FLAGYNCORSO  =  "S"
           then
      *        continue
               perform  A14-FINE-ELAB  thru  A14-EX
      *    else
      *        go  to  A10-EX
           end-if.
      *
       A10-EX.  exit.
      *
      *
       E45-STAMPA-RPT.
      *
           EVALUATE WTIPODOM
             WHEN "B"
               perform  E31-DETASU   thru  E31-DETASU-EX
             WHEN "D"
               perform  E32-DETLPU   thru  E32-DETLPU-EX
             WHEN "E"
               perform  E33-DETSX    thru  E33-DETSX-EX
           END-EVALUATE.
      *
      *   RECUPERI
      *
           perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
                    until NDR1            >  60
              IF EL-IMP-REC-A(NDR1) NOT = 0
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-DARE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
      *          MOVE EL-VOCE-REC(NDR1)      TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 STRING EL-ALF-REC-A(NDR1)
                        EL-NUM-REC-A(NDR1)(1:2)
                        EL-NUM-REC-A(NDR1)(4:3)
                  DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-KEY
                 PERFORM    E45-LEGGI-CONTO THRU E45-LEGGI-CONTO-EX
                 STRING EL-ALF-REC-A(NDR1) ' '
                        EL-NUM-REC-A(NDR1)(1:3)
                        EL-NUM-REC-A(NDR1)(4:3)
                 DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE EL-IMP-REC-A(NDR1)     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
                 MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 STRING '01' WK-RIGA-STAMPA   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                         INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 ADD 1                     TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
                 PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
              END-IF
           END-PERFORM.
      *
      *   SINDACATI AVERE
      *
           perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
      * SSS correttivo per sindacati da 10 03 in poi
160125*             until NDR1            >  300
160125              until NDR1            >  400
      * SSS-F
              IF EL-IMP-SIND-A(NDR1) NOT = 0
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-DARE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
      *          MOVE EL-VOCE-SIND(NDR1)      TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 STRING EL-ALF-SIND-A(NDR1)
                        EL-NUM-SIND-A(NDR1)(1:2)
                        EL-NUM-SIND-A(NDR1)(4:3)
                  DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-KEY
                 PERFORM    E45-LEGGI-CONTO THRU E45-LEGGI-CONTO-EX
                 STRING EL-ALF-SIND-A(NDR1) ' '
                        EL-NUM-SIND-A(NDR1)(1:3)
                        EL-NUM-SIND-A(NDR1)(4:3)
                 DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE EL-IMP-SIND-A(NDR1)     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
                 MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 STRING '01' WK-RIGA-STAMPA   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                         INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 ADD 1                     TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
                 PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
              END-IF
           END-PERFORM.
      *
      *   SINDACATI DARE  D
      *
           perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
      * SSS correttivo per sindacati da 10 03 in poi
160125*             until NDR1            >  300
160125              until NDR1            >  400
      * SSS-F
              IF EL-IMP-SIND-D(NDR1) NOT = 0
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-DARE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
      *          MOVE EL-VOCE-SIND(NDR1)      TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 STRING EL-ALF-SIND-D(NDR1)
                        EL-NUM-SIND-D(NDR1)(1:2)
                        EL-NUM-SIND-D(NDR1)(4:3)
                  DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-KEY
                 PERFORM    E45-LEGGI-CONTO THRU E45-LEGGI-CONTO-EX
                 STRING EL-ALF-SIND-D(NDR1) ' '
                        EL-NUM-SIND-D(NDR1)(1:3)
                        EL-NUM-SIND-D(NDR1)(4:3)
                 DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-DARE
                 MOVE EL-IMP-SIND-D(NDR1)     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
      *--
                 MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 STRING '01' WK-RIGA-STAMPA   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                         INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 ADD 1                     TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
                 PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
              END-IF
           END-PERFORM.
      *
      *   SINDACATI AVERE C
      *
           perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
      * SSS correttivo per sindacati da 10 03 in poi
160125*             until NDR1            >  300
160125              until NDR1            >  400
      * SSS-F
              IF EL-IMP-SIND-C(NDR1) NOT = 0
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-DARE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
      *          MOVE EL-VOCE-SIND(NDR1)      TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 STRING EL-ALF-SIND-C(NDR1)
                        EL-NUM-SIND-C(NDR1)(1:2)
                        EL-NUM-SIND-C(NDR1)(4:3)
                  DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-KEY
                 PERFORM    E45-LEGGI-CONTO THRU E45-LEGGI-CONTO-EX
                 STRING EL-ALF-SIND-C(NDR1) ' '
                        EL-NUM-SIND-C(NDR1)(1:3)
                        EL-NUM-SIND-C(NDR1)(4:3)
                 DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE EL-IMP-SIND-C(NDR1)     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
                 MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 STRING '01' WK-RIGA-STAMPA   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                         INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 ADD 1                     TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
                 PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
              END-IF
           END-PERFORM.
      *
           IF WK-APP-RECSPE NOT = 0
              MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-DARE
              MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
              MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
              MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
              MOVE "GPA24042"            TO WK-CONTO-KEY
              PERFORM    E45-LEGGI-CONTO THRU E45-LEGGI-CONTO-EX
              MOVE "GPA 24/042"          TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
              MOVE WK-APP-RECSPE         TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
              MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
              STRING '01' WK-RIGA-STAMPA   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                      INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
              ADD 1                     TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
              PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
           END-IF.
      *
           IF WK-APP-RECIVA NOT = 0
              MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-DARE
              MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
              MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
              MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
              MOVE "GPA24025"            TO WK-CONTO-KEY
              PERFORM    E45-LEGGI-CONTO THRU E45-LEGGI-CONTO-EX
              MOVE "GPA 24/025"          TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
              MOVE WK-APP-RECIVA         TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
              MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
              STRING '01' WK-RIGA-STAMPA   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                      INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
              ADD 1                     TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
              PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
              MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
           END-IF.
      *
      * RIGA ERRORI
      *
           perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
                    until NDR1            >  300
              IF ELE-RIGA-ERRORI(NDR1) NOT = SPACES
              THEN
                 MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 ADD 1                      TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
                 STRING '04' ELE-RIGA-ERRORI(NDR1) DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                          INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT  THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
              ELSE
                 MOVE 999                 TO NDR1
              END-IF
           end-perform.
      *
           perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
                    until NDR1            >  300
              IF  RIGA-STAMPA(NDR1) NOT = SPACES
              THEN
                 MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 ADD 1                      TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
                 MOVE RIGA-STAMPA(NDR1)     TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT  THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
              ELSE
                 MOVE 999                 TO NDR1
              END-IF
           end-perform.
      *
      * STAMPA BIGLIETTO CONTABILE 730
      *
      *17072020 eliminata perchè non si chiama più popwmain
      *    MOVE 0              TO  TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA.
      *    MOVE 19             TO  TDSREPORT-NUM-RPT.
      *
      *    perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
      *             until NDR1            >  100
      *       IF BC-IMPORTO-SIN-1(NDR1) > 0
      *       THEN
      *          MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-DARE
      *          MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
      *          MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
      *          MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *          MOVE BC-IMPORTO-SIN-1(NDR1)  TO R-BCA-IMPORTO(NDR1)
      *          MOVE BC-CODICE-CONTO-SIN-1(NDR1) TO WK-CONTO-KEY
      *          PERFORM    E45-LEGGI-CONTO THRU E45-LEGGI-CONTO-EX
      *          MOVE "/"                       TO WK-BARRA
      *          MOVE WK-CONTO1-KEY             TO WK-CONTO-ALF
      *          MOVE WK-CONTO2-KEY             TO WK-CONTO-NUM1
      *          MOVE WK-CONTO3-KEY             TO WK-CONTO-NUM2
      *          IF BC-FLAG-DARE-AVERE-SIN-1(NDR1)  = "D"
      *          THEN
      *             MOVE WK-CONTO              TO WK-CONTO-DARE
      *             MOVE R-BCA-IMPORTO(NDR1)   TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
      *             ADD  BC-IMPORTO-SIN-1(NDR1)  TO WK-TOT-DARE
      *          ELSE
      *             MOVE WK-CONTO              TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
      *             MOVE R-BCA-IMPORTO(NDR1)   TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *             ADD  BC-IMPORTO-SIN-1(NDR1)  TO WK-TOT-AVERE
      *          END-IF
      *          MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
      *          STRING '01' WK-RIGA-STAMPA   DELIMITED BY SIZE
      *                                  INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
      *          ADD 1                     TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
      *          PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
      *       ELSE
      *          MOVE 999                 TO NDR1
      *       END-IF
      *    end-perform.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
           IF WK-TOT-AVERE > 0
           then
              move WK-TOT-AVERE    to RTOTDA
              move WK-TOT-DARE     to RTOTAV
              ADD   1              TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
              MOVE SPACES          TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
              STRING '02' RWK-TOTALI   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                     INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
              PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
           END-IF.
      *
       E45-STAMPA-RPT-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       E45-LEGGI-CONTO.
      *
           MOVE WK-CONTO-KEY          TO H-CONNUMERO.
           PERFORM E45-DB2-SELECT     THRU E45-DB2-SELECT-EX.
           IF SQLCODE NOT = 0
              MOVE SPACES               TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
              STRING "Manca descrizione conto : "  WK-CONTO-KEY
                     DELIMITED BY SIZE  INTO WK-DESCR-CONTO
           ELSE
              MOVE H-CONDESCRI          TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
           END-IF.
      *
       E45-LEGGI-CONTO-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       A12-UPD-RIEPILOGO.
           move  L-PROCEDURA      to H-PPROCEDURA .
           move  L-CODICE-STOP    to H-PSTRUTTURA .
           move  "N"              to H-PBACKUP    .
           PERFORM A10-DB2-SELECT THRU A10-DB2-SELECT-EX.
           IF SQLCODE NOT = 0
               move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
               move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
               EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT ROLLBACK END-EXEC
               go  to A12-EX
           ELSE
               if  F-LRIEPILOGO  =    0
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
                   move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
                   EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT ROLLBACK END-EXEC
                   go  to A12-EX
               end-if
           end-IF.
      *
           move  W-BIGLIETTO to           H-PIMPCONTAB.
           move  W8-ODIERNA  to           H-PDATAEMISS.
           PERFORM A12-DB2-UPDATE THRU A12-DB2-UPDATE-EX.
           IF SQLCODE NOT = 0
               move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
               move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
               EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT ROLLBACK END-EXEC
           ELSE
               if  F-LRIEPILOGO  =    0
               then
                   EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT END-EXEC
               else
                   move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
                   move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
                   EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT ROLLBACK END-EXEC
               end-if
           end-IF.
       A12-EX.  exit.
      *
       A14-FINE-ELAB.
      *------------------------------------ Memorizzo fine elaboraz. *
           move  L-CODICE-SEDE    to  C-CODICE-SEDE.
           move  L-CODICE-STOP    to  C-CODICE-STOP.
           move  L-NOME-SEDE      to  C-NOME-SEDE.
           move  L-NOME-STOP      to  C-NOME-STOP.
           move  L-PROCEDURA      to  C-PROCEDURA.
           move  "F"              to  C-RICHIESTA.
           move  L-PROGRESSIVO    to  C-PROGRESSIVO.
           move  zeros            to  C-CONGUAGLIO.
           move  spaces           to  C-DIRIGENTE
                                      C-ELABINCORSO
                                      C-RETCODE.
      *
           call  PDSPD16
                  using  WDFHEIBLK  WDFHCOMMAREA
                         AREALINK-1  AREALINK-2
           end-call.
           cancel  PDSPD16 .
      *-------------------------------------- Elaborazione corretta?
           if  C-RETCODE      =  "C"   and
               C-ELABINCORSO  =  "K"
           then
               continue
           else
               move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
               perform  T76-TESTO76    thru  T76-EX
               perform  W10-MSGERRORE  thru  W10-EX
           end-if.
       A14-EX.  exit.
      *
      *
       A20-TELEMATICO.
      *
           move  L-CODICE-SEDE    to  C-CODICE-SEDE.
           move  L-CODICE-STOP    to  C-CODICE-STOP.
           move  L-NOME-SEDE      to  C-NOME-SEDE.
           move  L-NOME-STOP      to  C-NOME-STOP.
           move  L-PROCEDURA      to  C-PROCEDURA.
           move  L-RICHIESTA      to  C-RICHIESTA.
           move  L-PROGRESSIVO    to  C-PROGRESSIVO.
           move  zeros            to  C-CONGUAGLIO.
           move  spaces           to  C-DIRIGENTE
                                      C-ELABINCORSO
                                      C-RETCODE.
           move H-PDATAELABO   TO     WK-PDATAELABO.
      *
090523*    if  LMATRICOLA  =  "78360000"    and
      *        L-CODICE-SEDE  =  "0200"
      *    then
      *    display "NIK rdspd05,LMATRICOLA :   "  LMATRICOLA
      *    display "NIK rdspd05,W-BIGLIETTO:   "  W-BIGLIETTO
      *    display "NIK rdspd05,EL-TABINT1(1) :"  EL-TABINT1(1)
      *    display "NIK rdspd05,EL-TABINT1(2) :"  EL-TABINT1(2)
      *    display "NIK rdspd05,EL-TABINT1(3) :"  EL-TABINT1(3)
      *    display "NIK rdspd05,EL-TABINT1(4) :"  EL-TABINT1(4)
090523*    end-if.
      *
           call   RDSPD05   using
                 WDFHEIBLK  WDFHCOMMAREA
                 WK-PDATAELABO
                 H-PCODTELEMA
                 W-BIGLIETTO
                 AREALINK-1
                 LAREA-D
                 TABINT1
                 TAB-ERRORI
           end-call.
           cancel  RDSPD05 .
           if  C-RETCODE    =  "C"
           then  continue
           else  move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
       A20-EX.
           exit.
      *
       C00-CENTRALI.
           if  W-ERRORE  =  "S"
           then
               go  to  C00-EX
           end-if.
           if  L-RETCODE  =  "N"

       E50-BIGASU.
      * imposta data inizio e fine elaborazione per b.c. 730
           IF H-O0DCODTULSP < DAL-730
               MOVE H-O0DCODTULSP TO DAL-730
           END-IF.

               MOVE H-O0DCODTULSP TO AL-730
           END-IF.
      * controlla se presente INCENTIVO
           IF H-O0DCODTDESP > 20021231
           AND H-O0SUINCENT = "S"
           AND H-O0SUIMRIN > 9296,21

                   COMPUTE WK-RINUNCIA = H-O0SUIMRINU - 9296,22
                   MOVE 9296,22 TO WK-INCENTIVO
               ELSE
                   MOVE 0 TO WK-RINUNCIA
                   MOVE H-O0SUIMRINU TO WK-INCENTIVO
               END-IF
           ELSE
               MOVE H-O0SUIMRINU TO WK-RINUNCIA
               MOVE ZEROES TO WK-INCENTIVO
           END-IF.

               COMPUTE ALIQINC  rounded = H-O0SUIRPEFU /
                                 (WK-RINUNCIA + WK-INCENTIVO)
               COMPUTE ALIQINCR rounded = H-O0SUADDIZRR /
                                 (WK-RINUNCIA + WK-INCENTIVO)
               COMPUTE ALIQINCC rounded = H-O0SUADDIZRC /
                                 (WK-RINUNCIA + WK-INCENTIVO)
               COMPUTE WK-IRPEF-INC rounded            =
                       WK-INCENTIVO                    *
                     ( ALIQINC + ALIQINCR + ALIQINCC )
           END-IF.
      *
           COMPUTE WK-DEBITO = H-O0SUIMINU  +
                               H-O0SUIMRINU +
                               WK-IRPEF-INC -
                               WK-INCENTIVO -
                               H-O0SUIRPEFU -
                               H-O0SUTRASIND -
                               H-O0SUADDIZR -

           ELSE

      * conguaglio 730

                   ADD H-O0SUIMINU TO ASU    OF BIGASU-O
                   ADD H-O0RECIMURE1 TO ASU  OF BIGASU-O
      *            ADD H-O0RECIMURE3 TO ASU  OF BIGASU-O
               END-IF
           END-IF.
           IF H-O0SUMATASUT > 0
               IF H-O0SUEDIL = "S"
                   SUBTRACT H-O0SUMATASUU FROM ASUEDIL OF BIGASU-O
                   ADD H-O0SUMATASUU TO MATERNEDIL OF BIGASU-O
               ELSE
                   SUBTRACT H-O0SUMATASUU FROM ASU OF BIGASU-O
                   ADD H-O0SUMATASUU TO MATERNITA OF BIGASU-O
               END-IF
           END-IF.
           IF H-O0SUANFASUU < (H-O0SUIMANFU + H-O0RECIMURE2)
               IF H-O0SUEDIL = "S"
                   ADD H-O0SUANFASUU TO ANFEDIL OF BIGASU-O
               ELSE
                   ADD H-O0SUANFASUU TO ANFASU OF BIGASU-O
               END-IF
               ADD H-O0SUIMANFU   TO ANF75   OF BIGASU-O
               ADD H-O0RECIMURE2  TO ANF75   OF BIGASU-O
               SUBTRACT H-O0SUANFASUU FROM ANF75 OF BIGASU-O
           ELSE
               IF H-O0SUEDIL = "S"
                   ADD H-O0SUIMANFU TO ANFEDIL OF BIGASU-O
                   ADD H-O0RECIMURE2 TO ANFEDIL OF BIGASU-O
               ELSE
                   ADD H-O0SUIMANFU TO ANFASU OF BIGASU-O
                   ADD H-O0RECIMURE2 TO ANFASU OF BIGASU-O
               END-IF
           END-IF.
       E516-76.
           ADD H-O0SUIMINU    TO LPU76     OF BIGASU-O.
           ADD H-O0RECIMURE1  TO LPU76     OF BIGASU-O.
      *    ADD H-O0RECIMURE3  TO LPU76     OF BIGASU-O.
           IF H-O0SUMATASUT > 0
               SUBTRACT H-O0SUMATASUU FROM LPU76 OF BIGASU-O
               ADD H-O0SUMATASUU TO MATERNITA OF BIGASU-O
           END-IF.
           ADD H-O0SUIMANFU   TO ANF76     OF BIGASU-O.
           ADD H-O0RECIMURE2  TO ANF76     OF BIGASU-O.

                   H-O0SUMATASUU.
      *            MEZZO-ASU.

      *            (H-O0SUMATASUU - MEZZO-ASU).
                   H-O0SUMATASUU.

           ADD H-O0RECIMURE1 TO ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O.
      *    ADD H-O0RECIMURE3 TO ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O.
      * ho0sumatasuu x 2 perchè devo sottrarre importo intero maternità
           SUBTRACT H-O0SUMATASUU FROM ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O.
           SUBTRACT H-O0SUMATASUU FROM ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O.
           SUBTRACT H-O0SUIMASUU FROM ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O.
      *
           COMPUTE MEZZO-ANF = (H-O0SUIMANFU + H-O0RECIMURE2) / 2.
           COMPUTE ANFREG   OF BIGASU-O =
                   ANFREG   OF BIGASU-O +
                   MEZZO-ANF.
           COMPUTE ANFREGEG OF BIGASU-O =
                   ANFREGEG OF BIGASU-O +
                   (H-O0SUIMANFU + H-O0RECIMURE2) -
                   MEZZO-ANF.
      *
           COMPUTE DEBITI OF BIGASU-O =
                   DEBITI OF BIGASU-O +
                   (WK-DEBITO / 2).
           COMPUTE DEBITI OF BIGASU-O =
                   DEBITI OF BIGASU-O +
                   (H-O0SUIMANFU / 2).
      *
           COMPUTE MEZZO-ASU    = WK-DEBITO / 2.
           COMPUTE MEZZO-ANF    = H-O0SUIMANFU / 2.
           COMPUTE DEBASU OF BIGASU-O =
                   DEBASU OF BIGASU-O +
                   (WK-DEBITO - MEZZO-ASU).
           COMPUTE DEBASU OF BIGASU-O =
                   DEBASU OF BIGASU-O +
                   (H-O0SUIMANFU - MEZZO-ANF).

      * maternità

                   MATREGEG OF BIGASU-O +
                   (H-O0SUMATASUU * 1,5).
      * assegno asu
           ADD H-O0SUIMINU   TO ASUREGEG  OF BIGASU-O.
           ADD H-O0RECIMURE1 TO ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O.
      *    ADD H-O0RECIMURE3 TO ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O.
      * ho0sumatasuu x 2 perchè devo sottrarre importo intero maternità
           SUBTRACT H-O0SUMATASUU FROM ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O.
           COMPUTE ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O =
                   ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O -
                   (H-O0SUMATASUU * 1,5).
           SUBTRACT H-O0SUIMASUU FROM ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O.
      *
           ADD H-O0SUIMANFU  TO ANFREGEG OF BIGASU-O.
           ADD H-O0RECIMURE2 TO ANFREGEG OF BIGASU-O.
           SUBTRACT H-O0SUANFASUU FROM ANFREGEG OF BIGASU-O.

      *

                   DEBITI OF BIGASU-O +
                   DEBITO40X100.
           COMPUTE DEBITI OF BIGASU-O =
                   DEBITI OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANF40X100.
      *

                   DEBASU OF BIGASU-O +
                   WK-DEBITO -
                   DEBITO40X100.

                   DEBASU OF BIGASU-O +
                   H-O0SUIMANFU -
                   ANF40X100.

           ADD H-O0PUADDIZC TO ADDCOM   OF BIGLPU-O.

           ELSE

                       CONGRIMB OF BIGLPU-O +
                           H-O0PUCONGFIS * (-1)
           END-IF.

           ELSE
               COMPUTE RIMB730 OF BIGLPU-O =
                       RIMB730 OF BIGLPU-O +
                           H-O0PUCONG730 * (-1)
           END-IF.
      * trattenute sindacali

      * LAV. SOMMINISTRATI
           IF H-O0SXCODIND = "SOMM"
               COMPUTE EL-IMP-SX-D(142)               =
                       EL-IMP-SX-D(142)               +
      *        ((H-O0SXIMINU + H-O0RECIMURE1 + H-O0RECIMURE3) / 2)
               ((H-O0SXIMINU + H-O0RECIMURE1) / 2)
               COMPUTE EL-IMP-SX-D(IND-SX) =
                       EL-IMP-SX-D(IND-SX) -
      *        ((H-O0SXIMINU + H-O0RECIMURE1 + H-O0RECIMURE3) / 2)
               ((H-O0SXIMINU + H-O0RECIMURE1) / 2)

           IF H-O0SXCODIND = "SSEP"

           IF H-O0SXIMRIN > 0
           AND (   H-O0SXCODIND = "FTMD"
                OR H-O0SXCODIND = "FTAD"

                OR H-O0SXCODIND = "CRED"   )

           OR H-O0RECIMURE2 > 0
           OR H-O0RECIMURE3 > 0
               PERFORM CARICA-TABELLA-RECUPERI
           END-IF.
      * recuperi su anticipazione
      * correttivo per FTMD h_sstrecrin contiene contrib. correlata
           IF H-O0SXIMRIN > 0
           AND (   H-O0SXCODIND = "FTMD"
                OR H-O0SXCODIND = "FTAD"
270324          OR H-O0SXCODIND = "FSAD"
                OR H-O0SXCODIND = "CRED"   )
               ADD H-O0SXRECRIN TO EL-IMP-SX-A(146)
           END-IF.
      * irpef
           ADD H-O0SXIRPEFU TO EL-IMP-SX-A(147).
           SUBTRACT H-O0FAPIMPNET FROM EL-IMP-SX-A(147).
           ADD H-O0FAPIMPNET TO EL-IMP-SX-A(148).
      * conguaglio fiscale
           IF H-O0SXCONGFIS > 0
               ADD H-O0SXCONGFIS TO EL-IMP-SX-A(149)
           ELSE
               COMPUTE EL-IMP-SX-D(149)     =
                       EL-IMP-SX-D(149)     +
                           H-O0SXCONGFIS * (-1)
           END-IF.
      * addizionali
           ADD H-O0SXADDIZR TO EL-IMP-SX-A(150).
           ADD H-O0SXADDIZC TO EL-IMP-SX-A(151).
           ADD H-O0SXADDIZRR TO EL-IMP-SX-A(152).
           ADD H-O0SXADDIZRC TO EL-IMP-SX-A(153).

      * conguaglio 730
           IF H-O0SXCONG730 > 0
               ADD H-O0SXCONG730 TO EL-IMP-SX-A(154)
           ELSE
               COMPUTE EL-IMP-SX-D(154)    =
                       EL-IMP-SX-D(154)    +
                           H-O0SXCONG730 * (-1)
           END-IF.
      * trattenute sindacali
160125*fatte correzioni su gestione sindacati
           IF H-O0SXTRASIND > 0
               ADD W-SPERIS    TO RECSPE OF RIGASPE-O
               ADD W-IVA       TO RECIVA OF RIGAIVA-O
               COMPUTE TS-NETTA = H-O0SXTRASIND - (W-SPERIS + W-IVA)
160125*        IF H-O0SXTSCONF = 10
160125*        AND H-O0SXTSCAT > 01
      **SSS correttivo per sindacati da 10 03 in poi
160125*            ADD H-O0SXTRASIND TO EL-IMP-SIND-C(90)
160125*            ADD H-O0SXTRASIND TO EL-IMP-SIND-C(H-O0SXTSCAT + 98)
160125*            IF H-PDATAELABO < 20120101
      **               ADD H-O0SXTRASIND TO EL-IMP-SIND-A(90)
160125*                ADD H-O0SXTRASIND
160125*                    TO EL-IMP-SIND-A(H-O0SXTSCAT + 98)
      **               ADD TS-NETTA   TO EL-IMP-SIND-D(90)
160125*                ADD TS-NETTA
160125*                    TO EL-IMP-SIND-D(H-O0SXTSCAT + 98)
160125*            END-IF
      * SSS-F
160125*        ELSE
160125*            ADD H-O0SXTRASIND TO EL-IMP-SIND-C(H-O0SXTSCONF)
160125*            IF H-PDATAELABO < 20120101
160125*                ADD H-O0SXTRASIND TO EL-IMP-SIND-A(H-O0SXTSCONF)
160125*                ADD TS-NETTA   TO EL-IMP-SIND-D(H-O0SXTSCONF)
160125*            END-IF
160125*        END-IF

160125         MOVE 1  TO IND-SIND
160125         PERFORM UNTIL IND-SIND > 400
160125           IF H-O0SXTSCONF  = EL-COD-SIND(IND-SIND) AND
160125              H-O0SXTSCAT   = EL-CAT-SIND(IND-SIND)
160125                ADD H-O0SXTRASIND TO EL-IMP-SIND-C(IND-SIND)
160125                IF H-PDATAELABO < 20120101
160125                    ADD H-O0SXTRASIND  TO EL-IMP-SIND-A(IND-SIND)
160125                    ADD TS-NETTA       TO EL-IMP-SIND-D(IND-SIND)
160125                END-IF
160125           ELSE
160125             add 1    to ind-sind
160125           END-IF
160125         END-PERFORM

               ADD H-O0SXTRASIND TO TOTALE-CONT
               IF H-PDATAELABO < 20120101
                   ADD H-O0SXTRASIND TO TOTALE-ACCR
                   ADD TS-NETTA   TO TOTALE-DEBI
               END-IF
           END-IF.
      * 20/05/2014 Massimo
           perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
                    until NDR1            >  160
              IF EL-IMP-SX-D(NDR1) < 0
              THEN
      *           SUBTRACT EL-IMP-SX-D(NDR1) FROM TOTDA OF TOTALI-O
      *           SUBTRACT EL-IMP-SX-D(NDR1) FROM TOTAV OF TOTALI-O
                  COMPUTE EL-IMP-SX-A(NDR1) = EL-IMP-SX-A(NDR1)
                                            - EL-IMP-SX-D(NDR1)
                  MOVE 0 TO EL-IMP-SX-D(NDR1)
                  MOVE EL-ALF-SX-D(NDR1) TO EL-ALF-SX-A(NDR1)
                  MOVE EL-NUM-SX-D(NDR1) TO EL-NUM-SX-A(NDR1)
              END-IF
              IF EL-IMP-SX-A(NDR1) < 0
              THEN
      *           SUBTRACT EL-IMP-SX-A(NDR1) FROM TOTDA OF TOTALI-O
      *           SUBTRACT EL-IMP-SX-A(NDR1) FROM TOTAV OF TOTALI-O
                  COMPUTE EL-IMP-SX-D(NDR1) = EL-IMP-SX-D(NDR1)
                                            - EL-IMP-SX-A(NDR1)
                  MOVE 0 TO EL-IMP-SX-A(NDR1)
                  MOVE EL-ALF-SX-A(NDR1) TO EL-ALF-SX-D(NDR1)
                  MOVE EL-NUM-SX-A(NDR1) TO EL-NUM-SX-D(NDR1)
              END-IF
           end-perform.
       E71-EX.  exit.
      *------------------------------------------------------------
       E30-TOTALIZZA.
      *------------------------------------------------------------
           EVALUATE WTIPODOM
             WHEN "B"
               perform  E31-TOTASU   thru  E31-EX
             WHEN "D"
               perform  E32-TOTLPU   thru  E32-EX
             WHEN "E"
               perform  E33-TOTSX    thru  E33-EX
           END-EVALUATE.
       E30-EX.   exit.
      *------------------------------------------------------------
       E31-TOTASU.
      *------------------------------------------------------------
      *  Credito verso ente ASU cofinaziati fino al 30/06/2001
           MOVE ASUEGCOF OF BIGASU-O
             TO ACCERD   OF BIGASU-O
                ACCERA   OF BIGASU-O.
      *  Credito verso ente ASU cofinaziati dopo il 30/06/2001
      *    IF H-R2SINO NOT = "50"
           IF H-O0SUFIN NOT = 09
               COMPUTE ACCEGD   OF BIGASU-O   =
                       ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O +
                       MATREGEG OF BIGASU-O
               MOVE ACCEGD   OF BIGASU-O
                 TO ACCEGA   OF BIGASU-O
           END-IF.
      *  Credito verso Regione ASU cofinaziati dopo il 30/06/2001
           IF H-R2SINO = "NO"
           AND H-O0SUFIN NOT = 09
               COMPUTE ACCREGD OF BIGASU-O  =
                       ASUREG OF BIGASU-O +
                       ANFREG OF BIGASU-O +
                       MATREG OF BIGASU-O
               MOVE ACCREGD   OF BIGASU-O
                 TO ACCREGA   OF BIGASU-O
           END-IF.
      *  Credito verso Regione LAZIO  ASU cof. REGIONE/FONDO
      *    IF H-R2SINO = "50"
           IF H-O0SUFIN = 09
               COMPUTE ACCREGD OF BIGASU-O  =
                       ASUREGEG OF BIGASU-O +
                       ANFREGEG OF BIGASU-O +
                       MATREGEG OF BIGASU-O
               MOVE ACCREGD   OF BIGASU-O
                 TO ACCREGA   OF BIGASU-O
           END-IF.
      *  Credito verso ente ASU autofinaziati
           COMPUTE ACCEREGD OF BIGASU-O   =
                   ASUEGAUT OF BIGASU-O +
                   MATERNEG OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANFASUEG OF BIGASU-O.
           MOVE ACCEREGD OF BIGASU-O
             TO ACCEREGA OF BIGASU-O.
      *
           COMPUTE TOTDA     OF TOTALI-O   =
                   ASU       OF BIGASU-O +
                   ASUREG    OF BIGASU-O +
                   ASUREGEG  OF BIGASU-O +
                   ASUEGCOF  OF BIGASU-O +
                   ASUEGAUT  OF BIGASU-O +
                   ASUFORM1  OF BIGASU-O +
                   ASUFORM2  OF BIGASU-O +
                   ASUEDIL   OF BIGASU-O +
                   LSU71     OF BIGASU-O +
                   LSU72     OF BIGASU-O +
                   LSU73     OF BIGASU-O +
                   LPU74     OF BIGASU-O +
                   LPU75     OF BIGASU-O +
                   LPU76     OF BIGASU-O +
                   RIN       OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANTIC     OF BIGASU-O +
                   INCENTIVO OF BIGASU-O +
                   MATERNITA OF BIGASU-O +
                   MATREG    OF BIGASU-O +
                   MATREGEG  OF BIGASU-O +
                   MATERNEDIL OF BIGASU-O +
                   MATERNEG  OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANFASU    OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANFREG    OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANFREGEG  OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANFASUEG  OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANFFORM1  OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANFFORM2  OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANFEDIL   OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANF71     OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANF72     OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANF73     OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANF74     OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANF75     OF BIGASU-O +
                   ANF76     OF BIGASU-O +
                   CONGRIMB  OF BIGASU-O   +
                   RIMB730   OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ACCERD    OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ACCEREGD  OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ACCREGD   OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ACCEGD    OF BIGASU-O   +
                   TOTALE-ACCR
           on  size  error
               move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
           end-compute.
      *
           COMPUTE TOTAV     OF TOTALI-O   =
                   RECU      OF BIGASU-O +
                   RECURIN   OF BIGASU-O +
                   RECUANT   OF BIGASU-O +
                   IRPEF     OF BIGASU-O   +
                   IRPEFS    OF BIGASU-O   +
                   CONGDEB   OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ADDREG    OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ADDCOM    OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ADDREGR   OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ADDCOMR   OF BIGASU-O   +
                   DEB730    OF BIGASU-O   +
                   DEBITI    OF BIGASU-O   +
                   DEBASU    OF BIGASU-O   +
                   DEBITIEG  OF BIGASU-O   +
                   DEBITIINC OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ACCERA    OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ACCEREGA  OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ACCREGA   OF BIGASU-O   +
                   ACCEGA    OF BIGASU-O   +
                   TOTALE-CONT             +
                   TOTALE-DEBI             +
                   RECSPE    OF RIGASPE-O   +
                   RECIVA    OF RIGAIVA-O
           on  size  error
               move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
           end-compute.
      *
           COMPUTE W-BIGLIETTO = DEBITI    OF BIGASU-O   +
                                 DEBASU    OF BIGASU-O   +
                                 DEBITIEG  OF BIGASU-O   +
                                 DEBITIINC OF BIGASU-O.
      *
           COMPUTE STORNO    OF STORNO-O    =
                   RECU      OF BIGASU-O +
                   RECURIN   OF BIGASU-O +
                   RECUANT   OF BIGASU-O.
           MOVE STORNO OF STORNO-O TO TOTALE OF STORNO-O.
       E31-EX.   exit.
      *
       E31-DETASU.
      *
           MOVE 0              TO  TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA.
      *
           perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
                    until NDR1            >  70
              IF EL-IMP-ASU-D(NDR1) > 0
              THEN
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-DARE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
                 MOVE EL-VOCE-ASU(NDR1)      TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 STRING EL-ALF-ASU-D(NDR1) ' '
                        EL-NUM-ASU-D(NDR1)
                        EL-NUM-ASU-D(NDR1)
                 DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-DARE
                 MOVE EL-IMP-ASU-D(NDR1)     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
      *--
                 IF WK-CONTO-DARE = 'GPA 06/105'
                    MOVE 'CREDITO IRPEF DA CONGUAGLIO FISCALE          '
                       TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 END-IF
      *--
                 MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 STRING '01' WK-RIGA-STAMPA   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                         INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 ADD 1                     TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
                 PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
              END-IF
           end-perform.
      *
           perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
                    until NDR1            >  70
              IF EL-IMP-ASU-A(NDR1) > 0
              THEN
      *--
                IF EL-ALF-ASU-A(NDR1) = 'GPA' AND
                   EL-NUM-ASU-A(NDR1) = '52/099'
                THEN
                   MOVE 1            TO SW-RECUPERI
                ELSE
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-DARE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
                 MOVE EL-VOCE-ASU(NDR1)      TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 STRING EL-ALF-ASU-A(NDR1) ' '
                        EL-NUM-ASU-A(NDR1)
                        EL-NUM-ASU-A(NDR1)
                 DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE EL-IMP-ASU-A(NDR1)     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
                 IF WK-CONTO-AVERE = 'GPA 29/105'
                    MOVE 'DEBITO IRPEF DA CONGUAGLIO FISCALE           '
                       TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 END-IF
      *--
                 MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 STRING '01' WK-RIGA-STAMPA   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                         INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 ADD 1                     TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
                 PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
                END-IF
              END-IF
           end-perform.
       E31-DETASU-EX.     exit.

       E32-TOTLPU.
      *------------------------------------------------------------
           COMPUTE TOTDA     OF TOTALI-O   =
                   LPU280I   OF BIGLPU-O +
                   LPU280R   OF BIGLPU-O +
                   MATERNITA OF BIGLPU-O +
                   ANF280I   OF BIGLPU-O +
                   ANF280R   OF BIGLPU-O +
                   CONGRIMB  OF BIGLPU-O   +
                   RIMB730   OF BIGLPU-O   +
                   TOTALE-ACCR
           on  size  error
               move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
           end-compute.
      *
           COMPUTE TOTAV     OF TOTALI-O   =
                   RECU      OF BIGLPU-O +
                   IRPEF     OF BIGLPU-O   +
                   IRPEFS    OF BIGLPU-O   +
                   CONGDEB   OF BIGLPU-O   +
                   ADDREG    OF BIGLPU-O   +
                   ADDCOM    OF BIGLPU-O   +
                   DEB730    OF BIGLPU-O   +
                   DEBITI    OF BIGLPU-O   +
                   TOTALE-CONT              +
                   TOTALE-DEBI              +
                   RECSPE    OF RIGASPE-O   +
                   RECIVA    OF RIGAIVA-O
           on  size  error
               move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
           end-compute.
      *
           COMPUTE W-BIGLIETTO = DEBITI OF BIGLPU-O.
      *
           COMPUTE STORNO    OF STORNO-O    =
                   RECU      OF BIGLPU-O.
           MOVE STORNO OF STORNO-O TO TOTALE OF STORNO-O.
       E32-EX.   exit.

      *--

                        EL-NUM-LPU-A(NDR1)
                        EL-NUM-LPU-A(NDR1)
                 DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE EL-IMP-LPU-A(NDR1)     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE

      *------------------------------------------------------------
       E33-TOTSX.
      *------------------------------------------------------------
           MOVE 0 TO TOTDA OF TOTALI-O
                     TOTAV OF TOTALI-O.
           MOVE 1 TO IND-SX.
           PERFORM UNTIL IND-SX > 160
               ADD EL-IMP-SX-D(IND-SX) TO TOTDA OF TOTALI-O
               on  size  error
                   move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
               END-ADD
               ADD EL-IMP-SX-A(IND-SX) TO TOTAV OF TOTALI-O
               on  size  error
                   move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
               END-ADD
               ADD 1 TO IND-SX
           END-PERFORM.
      *
           COMPUTE TOTDA     OF TOTALI-O    =
                   TOTDA     OF TOTALI-O    +
                   TOTALE-ACCR
           on  size  error
               move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
           end-compute.
      *
           COMPUTE TOTAV     OF TOTALI-O    =
                   TOTAV     OF TOTALI-O    +
                   TOTALE-CONT              +
                   TOTALE-DEBI              +
                   RECSPE    OF RIGASPE-O   +
                   RECIVA    OF RIGAIVA-O
           on  size  error
               move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
           end-compute.
      *
           COMPUTE W-BIGLIETTO = EL-IMP-SX-A(155)         +
                                 EL-IMP-SX-A(156)         +
                                 EL-IMP-SX-A(157)         +
                                 EL-IMP-SX-A(158).
      *
           COMPUTE STORNO    OF STORNO-O   =
                   EL-IMP-SX-A(145)        +
                   EL-IMP-SX-A(146).
           MOVE STORNO OF STORNO-O TO TOTALE OF STORNO-O.
       E33-EX.   exit.
      *
       E33-DETSX.
      *
           MOVE 0              TO  TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA.
      *
           perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
                    until NDR1            >  160
              IF EL-IMP-SX-D(NDR1) > 0
              THEN
      *--
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-DARE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
                 MOVE EL-VOCE-SX(NDR1)      TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 STRING EL-ALF-SX-D(NDR1) ' '
                        EL-NUM-SX-D(NDR1)
                        EL-NUM-SX-D(NDR1)
                 DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-DARE
                 MOVE EL-IMP-SX-D(NDR1)     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
      *--
                 IF WK-CONTO-DARE = 'GPA 06/105'
                    MOVE 'CREDITO IRPEF DA CONGUAGLIO FISCALE          '
                       TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 END-IF
      *--
                 MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 STRING '01' WK-RIGA-STAMPA   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                         INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 ADD 1                     TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
                 PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
              END-IF
           end-perform.
      *
      *
           perform  varying  NDR1  from  1  by  1
                    until NDR1            >  160
              IF EL-IMP-SX-A(NDR1) > 0
              THEN
      *--
                IF EL-ALF-SX-A(NDR1) = 'GPA' AND
                   EL-NUM-SX-A(NDR1) = '52/099'
                THEN
                   MOVE 1            TO SW-RECUPERI
                ELSE
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-DARE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-DARE
                 MOVE SPACES                TO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE 0                     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
                 MOVE EL-VOCE-SX(NDR1)      TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 STRING EL-ALF-SX-A(NDR1) ' '
                        EL-NUM-SX-A(NDR1)
                        EL-NUM-SX-A(NDR1)
                 DELIMITED BY SIZE        INTO WK-CONTO-AVERE
                 MOVE EL-IMP-SX-A(NDR1)     TO WK-IMPOR-AVERE
      *--
                 IF WK-CONTO-AVERE = 'GPA 29/105'
                    MOVE 'DEBITO IRPEF DA CONGUAGLIO FISCALE           '
                       TO WK-DESCR-CONTO
                 END-IF
      *--
                 MOVE SPACES               TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 STRING '01' WK-RIGA-STAMPA   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                         INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                 ADD 1                     TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
                 PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
                END-IF
              END-IF
           end-perform.
       E33-DETSX-EX.     exit.
      *------------------------------------------------------------
       STAMPA-BIGLIETTO.
      *
      *------------------------------------------------ Prima   pagina
           move  L-PROGRESSIVO  to  S5BBB1N of TESTASU-O
                                    S5BBB1N of TESTLPU-O
                                    S5BBB1N of TESTSX-O.
      *
           move  L-NOME-SEDE    to  S5B101A of TESTASU-O
                                    S5B101A of TESTLPU-O
                                    S5B101A of TESTSX-O.
           move  L-CODICE-STOP  to  S5N101S of TESTASU-O
                                    S5N101S of TESTLPU-O
                                    S5N101S of TESTSX-O.
           move  L-NOME-STOP    to  S5A101S of TESTASU-O
                                    S5A101S of TESTLPU-O
                                    S5A101S of TESTSX-O.
      *
           EVALUATE WTIPODOM
             WHEN "B"
                 PERFORM STAMPA-ASU
             WHEN "D"
                 PERFORM STAMPA-LPU
             WHEN "E"
                 PERFORM STAMPA-SX
           END-EVALUATE.
      *
           PERFORM STAMPA-SINDACATI.
      *
      * gestione recuperi
           PERFORM STAMPA-RECUPERI.
      *
           PERFORM STAMPA-TOTALI.
      *
      *    if  STORNO OF STORNO-O >  zeroes
           if  SW-RECUPERI = 1
           then
               MOVE STORNO           TO RSTORNO
               MOVE TOTALE           TO RTOTALE
               MOVE SPACES           TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
               STRING '03' WK-BIGSTORNO-04   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                                   INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
               ADD   1               TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
               MOVE TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT        TO
                    RIGA-STAMPA(2)
           end-if.
       EX-BIGLIETTO.  exit.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
       STAMPA-ASU.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
           MOVE ASU           OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(1).
           IF H-O0SUFIN = 09
               MOVE ASUREG    OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(2)
               MOVE ASUREGEG  OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(57)
           ELSE
               IF H-R2SINO = "SI"
                   MOVE ASUREG    OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(2)
               END-IF
               IF H-R2SINO = "NO"
                   MOVE ASUREG    OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(3)
               END-IF
               MOVE ASUREGEG      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(4)
           END-IF.
           MOVE ASUEGCOF      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(5).
           MOVE ASUEGAUT      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(6).
           MOVE ASUFORM1      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(7).
           MOVE ASUFORM2      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(8).
           MOVE ASUEDIL       OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(9).
           MOVE LSU71         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(10).
           MOVE LSU72         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(11).
           MOVE LSU73         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(12).
           MOVE LPU74         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(13).
           MOVE LPU75         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(14).
           MOVE LPU76         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(15).
           MOVE RIN           OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(16).
           MOVE ANTIC         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(17).
           MOVE INCENTIVO     OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(18).
           MOVE MATERNITA     OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(19).
           IF H-O0SUFIN = 09
               MOVE MATREG    OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(20)
               MOVE MATREGEG  OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(58)
           ELSE
               IF H-R2SINO = "SI"
                   MOVE MATREG    OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(20)
               END-IF
               IF H-R2SINO = "NO"
                   MOVE MATREG    OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(21)
               END-IF
               MOVE MATREGEG  OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(22)
           END-IF.
           MOVE MATERNEDIL    OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(23).
           MOVE MATERNEG      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(24).
           MOVE ANFASU        OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(25).
           IF H-O0SUFIN = 09
               MOVE ANFREG    OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(26)
               MOVE ANFREGEG  OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(59)
           ELSE
               IF H-R2SINO = "SI"
                   MOVE ANFREG    OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(26)
               END-IF
               IF H-R2SINO = "NO"
                   MOVE ANFREG    OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(27)
               END-IF
           END-IF.
           MOVE ANFASUEG      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(28).
           MOVE ANFFORM1      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(29).
           MOVE ANFFORM2      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(30).
           MOVE ANFEDIL       OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(31).
           MOVE ANF71         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(32).
           MOVE ANF72         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(33).
           MOVE ANF73         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(34).
           MOVE ANF74         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(35).
           MOVE ANF75         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(36).
           MOVE ANF76         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(37).
           MOVE RECU          OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(38).
           MOVE RECURIN       OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(39).
           MOVE RECUANT       OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(40).
           IF WK-INCENTIVO > 0 AND < 9296,22
               MOVE "RECUPERI SU INCENTIVO DEC.MIN. 21/5/98       "
                 TO EL-VOCE-ASU(40)
               MOVE "GAU"                 TO EL-ALF-ASU-A(40)
               MOVE "24/046"              TO EL-NUM-ASU-A(40)
               MOVE RECUINC   OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(40)
           END-IF.
      *
           MOVE IRPEF         OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(41).
           MOVE IRPEFS        OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(42).
           MOVE CONGDEB       OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(43).
           MOVE CONGRIMB      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(43).
           MOVE ADDREG        OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(44).
           MOVE ADDCOM        OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(45).
           MOVE ADDREGR       OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(46).
           MOVE ADDCOMR       OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(47).
           MOVE DEB730        OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(48).
           MOVE RIMB730       OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-D(48).
           MOVE DEBITI        OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(49).
      * Su indicazione D.ssa Di Cecca per cofinanz. Reg. Lazio
      * il debito vs i lavoratori sullo stesso conto del FO
           IF H-O0SUFIN = 09
               ADD  DEBASU        OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(49)
           ELSE
               MOVE DEBASU        OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(50)
           END-IF.
           MOVE DEBITIEG      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(51).
           MOVE DEBITIINC     OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(52).
           MOVE ACCERD        OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(53)
                                             EL-IMP-ASU-D(53).
           MOVE ACCEREGD      OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(54)
                                             EL-IMP-ASU-D(54).
           IF H-O0SUFIN = 09
               MOVE ACCREGD       OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(60)
                                                 EL-IMP-ASU-D(60)
           ELSE
               MOVE ACCREGD       OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(55)
                                                 EL-IMP-ASU-D(55)
           END-IF.
           MOVE ACCEGD        OF BIGASU-O TO EL-IMP-ASU-A(56)
                                             EL-IMP-ASU-D(56).
      *
           MOVE 1 TO IND-ASU.
           PERFORM STAMPA-RIGA-ASU UNTIL IND-ASU > 70.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
       STAMPA-RIGA-ASU.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
           IF EL-IMP-ASU-D(IND-ASU) NOT = 0
           OR EL-IMP-ASU-A(IND-ASU) NOT = 0
               MOVE EL-VOCE-ASU(IND-ASU)        TO VOCE
               MOVE EL-ALF-ASU-D(IND-ASU)       TO ALFDA
               MOVE EL-NUM-ASU-D(IND-ASU)       TO NUMDA
               MOVE EL-IMP-ASU-D(IND-ASU)       TO IMPDA
               MOVE EL-ALF-ASU-A(IND-ASU)       TO ALFAV
               MOVE EL-NUM-ASU-A(IND-ASU)       TO NUMAV
               MOVE EL-99-ASU-A(IND-ASU)        TO NOVENOVE
               MOVE EL-IMP-ASU-A(IND-ASU)       TO IMPAV
               ADD 1 TO CONTA-RIGHE
      * gestione recuperi
               IF IND-ASU NOT = 38
                   PERFORM SCRIVI-TABINT1
               END-IF
           END-IF.
           INITIALIZE WK-RIGA.
           ADD 1 TO IND-ASU.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
       STAMPA-LPU.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
           MOVE LPU280I       OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-D(1).
           MOVE LPU280R       OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-D(2).
           MOVE MATERNITA     OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-D(3).
           MOVE ANF280I       OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-D(4).
           MOVE ANF280R       OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-D(5).
           MOVE RECU          OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-A(6).
           MOVE DEBITI        OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-A(7).
           MOVE IRPEF         OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-A(8).
           MOVE IRPEFS        OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-A(9).
           MOVE CONGRIMB      OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-D(10).
           MOVE CONGDEB       OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-A(10).
           MOVE ADDREG        OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-A(11).
           MOVE ADDCOM        OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-A(12).
           MOVE RIMB730       OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-D(13).
           MOVE DEB730        OF BIGLPU-O TO EL-IMP-LPU-A(13).
      *
           MOVE 1 TO IND-LPU.
           PERFORM STAMPA-RIGA-LPU UNTIL IND-LPU > 15.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
       STAMPA-RIGA-LPU.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
           IF EL-IMP-LPU-D(IND-LPU) NOT = 0
           OR EL-IMP-LPU-A(IND-LPU) NOT = 0
               MOVE EL-VOCE-LPU(IND-LPU)        TO VOCE
               MOVE EL-ALF-LPU-D(IND-LPU)       TO ALFDA
               MOVE EL-NUM-LPU-D(IND-LPU)       TO NUMDA
               MOVE EL-IMP-LPU-D(IND-LPU)       TO IMPDA
               MOVE EL-ALF-LPU-A(IND-LPU)       TO ALFAV
               MOVE EL-NUM-LPU-A(IND-LPU)       TO NUMAV
               MOVE EL-99-LPU-A(IND-LPU)        TO NOVENOVE
               MOVE EL-IMP-LPU-A(IND-LPU)       TO IMPAV
               ADD 1 TO CONTA-RIGHE
      * gestione recuperi
               IF IND-LPU NOT = 6
                   PERFORM SCRIVI-TABINT1
               END-IF
           END-IF.
           INITIALIZE WK-RIGA.
           ADD 1 TO IND-LPU.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
       STAMPA-SX.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
           MOVE 1 TO IND-SX.
           PERFORM STAMPA-RIGA-SX UNTIL IND-SX > 160.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
       STAMPA-RIGA-SX.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
           IF EL-IMP-SX-D(IND-SX) NOT = 0
           OR EL-IMP-SX-A(IND-SX) NOT = 0
               MOVE EL-VOCE-SX(IND-SX)        TO VOCE
               MOVE EL-ALF-SX-D(IND-SX)       TO ALFDA
               MOVE EL-NUM-SX-D(IND-SX)       TO NUMDA
               MOVE EL-IMP-SX-D(IND-SX)       TO IMPDA
               MOVE EL-ALF-SX-A(IND-SX)       TO ALFAV
               MOVE EL-NUM-SX-A(IND-SX)       TO NUMAV
               MOVE EL-99-SX-A(IND-SX)        TO NOVENOVE
               MOVE EL-IMP-SX-A(IND-SX)       TO IMPAV
               ADD 1 TO CONTA-RIGHE
      * gestione recuperi
               IF IND-SX NOT = 145
                   PERFORM SCRIVI-TABINT1
               END-IF
           END-IF.
           INITIALIZE WK-RIGA.
           ADD 1 TO IND-SX.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
       STAMPA-SINDACATI.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
           MOVE 1 TO IND-SIND.
      * SSS correttivo per sindacati da 10 03 in poi
      *    PERFORM UNTIL IND-SIND > 90
160125*    PERFORM UNTIL IND-SIND > 300
160125     PERFORM UNTIL IND-SIND > 400
      * SSS-F
               IF EL-IMP-SIND-A(IND-SIND) NOT = 0
                   STRING "ACCREDITAMENTO CONTRIBUTI SINDACALI "
                              DELIMITED BY SIZE
                          EL-VOCE-SIND(IND-SIND) DELIMITED BY SIZE
                     INTO VOCE
                   MOVE EL-ALF-SIND-A(IND-SIND)      TO ALFDA
                   MOVE EL-NUM-SIND-A(IND-SIND)      TO NUMDA
                   MOVE EL-IMP-SIND-A(IND-SIND)      TO IMPDA
                   MOVE SPACES                       TO ALFAV
                   MOVE SPACES                       TO NUMAV
                   MOVE SPACES                       TO NOVENOVE
                   MOVE ZEROES                       TO IMPAV
                   ADD 1 TO CONTA-RIGHE
                   PERFORM SCRIVI-TABINT1
               END-IF
               INITIALIZE WK-RIGA
               ADD 1 TO IND-SIND
           END-PERFORM.
      *
           MOVE 1 TO IND-SIND.
      * SSS correttivo per sindacati da 10 03 in poi
      *    PERFORM UNTIL IND-SIND > 90
160125*    PERFORM UNTIL IND-SIND > 300
160125     PERFORM UNTIL IND-SIND > 400
      * SSS-F
               IF EL-IMP-SIND-C(IND-SIND) NOT = 0
                   STRING "CONTRIBUTI SINDACALI " DELIMITED BY SIZE
                          EL-VOCE-SIND(IND-SIND)  DELIMITED BY SIZE
                     INTO VOCE
                   MOVE SPACES                       TO ALFDA
                   MOVE SPACES                       TO NUMDA
                   MOVE ZEROES                       TO IMPDA
                   MOVE EL-ALF-SIND-C(IND-SIND)      TO ALFAV
                   MOVE EL-NUM-SIND-C(IND-SIND)      TO NUMAV
                   MOVE SPACES                       TO NOVENOVE
                   MOVE EL-IMP-SIND-C(IND-SIND)      TO IMPAV
                   ADD 1 TO CONTA-RIGHE
                   PERFORM SCRIVI-TABINT1
               END-IF
               INITIALIZE WK-RIGA
               ADD 1 TO IND-SIND
           END-PERFORM.
      *
           MOVE 1 TO IND-SIND.
      * SSS correttivo per sindacati da 10 03 in poi
      *    PERFORM UNTIL IND-SIND > 90
160125*    PERFORM UNTIL IND-SIND > 300
160125     PERFORM UNTIL IND-SIND > 400
      * SSS-F
               IF EL-IMP-SIND-D(IND-SIND) NOT = 0
                   STRING "DEBITO VERSO "        DELIMITED BY SIZE
                          EL-VOCE-SIND(IND-SIND) DELIMITED BY SIZE
                     INTO VOCE
                   MOVE SPACES                       TO ALFDA
                   MOVE SPACES                       TO NUMDA
                   MOVE ZEROES                       TO IMPDA
                   MOVE EL-ALF-SIND-D(IND-SIND)      TO ALFAV
                   MOVE EL-NUM-SIND-D(IND-SIND)      TO NUMAV
                   MOVE SPACES                       TO NOVENOVE
                   MOVE EL-IMP-SIND-D(IND-SIND)      TO IMPAV
                   ADD 1 TO CONTA-RIGHE
                   PERFORM SCRIVI-TABINT1
               END-IF
               INITIALIZE WK-RIGA
               ADD 1 TO IND-SIND
           END-PERFORM.
      *
           IF RECSPE OF RIGASPE-O NOT = 0
               ADD 1 TO CONTA-RIGHE
               PERFORM SCRIVI-TABINT1-SPE
           END-IF.
           INITIALIZE WK-RIGASPE.
           IF RECIVA OF RIGAIVA-O NOT = 0
               ADD 1 TO CONTA-RIGHE
               PERFORM SCRIVI-TABINT1-IVA
           END-IF.
           INITIALIZE WK-RIGAIVA.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
      * gestione recuperi
       STAMPA-RECUPERI.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
           MOVE 1 TO IND-REC.
           PERFORM UNTIL IND-REC > 200
               IF EL-IMP-REC-A(IND-REC) NOT = 0
                   MOVE SPACES TO VOCE
                   MOVE "RECUPERI" TO VOCE
                   MOVE SPACES                      TO ALFDA
                   MOVE SPACES                      TO NUMDA
                   MOVE ZEROES                      TO IMPDA
                   MOVE EL-ALF-REC-A(IND-REC)       TO ALFAV
                   MOVE EL-NUM-REC-A(IND-REC)       TO NUMAV
                   MOVE SPACES                      TO NOVENOVE
                   MOVE EL-IMP-REC-A(IND-REC)       TO IMPAV
                   PERFORM SCRIVI-TABINT1
               END-IF
               ADD 1 TO IND-REC
           END-PERFORM.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
       STAMPA-TOTALI.
      *-----------------------------------------------------------*
           move   TOTDA         to RTOTDA.
           move   TOTAV         to RTOTAV.
           ADD   1           TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA.
           STRING '02' RWK-TOTALI   DELIMITED BY SIZE
                           INTO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT.
           MOVE TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT        TO
                RIGA-STAMPA(1).

       F00-FINALI.
           if  L-NOME-SEDE    =  "VALTOZAC"
           then  goback
           end-if.
      *
           perform  E45-STAMPA-RPT    thru  E45-STAMPA-RPT-EX.
      *
           if  OUT-STATUS = '96' OR OUT-STATUS = '99'
           then
              move   VO-DSPFM034  to  OUT-MESSAGGIO
           ELSE
              IF W-ERRORE = "S"
              move   "91"             TO OUT-STATUS
              STRING
                 WK-RPT-KEY "Squadratura Biglietto Cont."
              DELIMITED BY SIZE INTO OUT-MESSAGGIO
           ELSE
              move   "00"             TO OUT-STATUS
              move   WK-RPT-KEY   TO OUT-MESSAGGIO
           end-if.

      *        MOVE "01" TO H-SINCATSIN

      *        IF SQLCODE  = 0
      *            MOVE H-SINCODSIN   TO EL-COD-SIND(IND-SIND)
      *            MOVE H-SINDENSIN   TO EL-VOCE-SIND(IND-SIND)

      *            END-IF

      *            MOVE W-CONNUM-A(3:3) TO W-CONTO(4:3)

      *            MOVE 0           TO EL-IMP-SIND-C(IND-SIND)

      *            MOVE W-CONNUM-A(3:3) TO W-CONTO(4:3)

160125         MOVE WK-SINCATSIN (2:2) TO H-SINCATSIN
               PERFORM I25-DB2-SELECT THRU I25-DB2-SELECT-EX
               IF SQLCODE = 0
                 IF H-SINCONALF1 not = "XXX"
                   MOVE H-SINCODSIN TO EL-COD-SIND(IND-SIND)
160125             MOVE H-SINCATSIN TO EL-CAT-SIND(IND-SIND)
                   MOVE H-SINDENSIN TO EL-VOCE-SIND(IND-SIND)
                   MOVE H-SINCONALF1 TO EL-ALF-SIND-A(IND-SIND)
                   MOVE H-SINCONNUM1 TO W-CONNUM-N
                   MOVE W-CONNUM-A(1:2) TO W-CONTO(1:2)
                   MOVE W-CONNUM-A(3:3) TO W-CONTO(4:3)
                   MOVE W-CONTO TO EL-NUM-SIND-A(IND-SIND)
                   MOVE 0       TO EL-IMP-SIND-A(IND-SIND)
                   MOVE H-SINCONALF2 TO EL-ALF-SIND-C(IND-SIND)
                   MOVE H-SINCONNUM2 TO W-CONNUM-N
                   MOVE W-CONNUM-A(1:2) TO W-CONTO(1:2)
                   MOVE W-CONNUM-A(3:3) TO W-CONTO(4:3)

                   MOVE 0       TO EL-IMP-SIND-C(IND-SIND)

                   MOVE H-SINCONNUM3 TO W-CONNUM-N

                   MOVE W-CONNUM-A(3:3) TO W-CONTO(4:3)

                   MOVE 0       TO EL-IMP-SIND-D(IND-SIND)
      *        display 'EL-COD-SIND(IND-SIND): '   EL-COD-SIND(IND-SIND)
      *        display 'EL-CAT-SIND(IND-SIND): '   EL-CAT-SIND(IND-SIND)
                 END-IF
160125           ADD 1 TO IND-SIND
160125           ADD 1 TO WK-SINCATSIN
               ELSE
160125             ADD  1 TO WK-SINCODSIN
160125             MOVE 1 TO WK-SINCATSIN

160125*            MOVE IND-SIND    TO EL-COD-SIND(IND-SIND)
160125*            MOVE SPACES      TO EL-VOCE-SIND(IND-SIND)

160125*            MOVE SPACES      TO EL-ALF-SIND-D(IND-SIND)
160125*            MOVE SPACES      TO EL-NUM-SIND-D(IND-SIND)
160125*            MOVE 0           TO EL-IMP-SIND-D(IND-SIND)
               END-IF
160125*        MOVE 10 TO WK-SINCODSIN
160125*        ADD 1 TO WK-SINCATSIN

           END-PERFORM.
