           move  "N"              to  W-FLAGYNCORSO.
      *------------------------------------ Memorizzo esecuzione
           move  L-CODICE-SEDE    to  C-CODICE-SEDE.
           move  L-CODICE-STOP    to  C-CODICE-STOP.
           move  L-NOME-SEDE      to  C-NOME-SEDE.
           move  L-NOME-STOP      to  C-NOME-STOP.
           move  L-PROCEDURA      to  C-PROCEDURA.
           move  "E"              to  C-RICHIESTA.
           move  L-PROGRESSIVO    to  C-PROGRESSIVO.
           move  zeros            to  C-CONGUAGLIO.
           move  spaces           to  C-DIRIGENTE
                                      C-ELABINCORSO
                                      C-RETCODE.
      *
           call  PDSPD16 USING
                     WDFHEIBLK  WDFHCOMMAREA
                     AREALINK-1  AREALINK-2
           end-call.
           cancel  PDSPD16 .
      *-------------------------------------- Elaborazione possibile?
           if  C-RETCODE      =  "C"   and
               C-ELABINCORSO  =  "Y"
           then
               move  "S"  to  W-FLAGYNCORSO
           else
               move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
               perform  T76-TESTO76    thru  T76-EX
               perform  W10-MSGERRORE thru  W10-EX
           end-if.
       I60-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       I70-DATISTRUTTURA.
           move  L-CODICE-SEDE  to  C-CODICE-SEDE.
           move  L-CODICE-STOP  to  C-CODICE-STOP.
           move  L-NOME-SEDE    to  C-NOME-SEDE.
           move  L-NOME-STOP    to  C-NOME-STOP.
           move  L-PROCEDURA    to  C-PROCEDURA.
           move  "I"            to  C-RICHIESTA.
           move  zeros          to  C-PROGRESSIVO
                                    C-CONGUAGLIO.
           move  spaces         to  C-DIRIGENTE
                                    C-ELABINCORSO
                                    C-RETCODE.
      *
           call  PDSPD16 USING
                     WDFHEIBLK  WDFHCOMMAREA
                     AREALINK-1  AREALINK-2
           end-call.
           cancel  PDSPD16 .
           if  C-RETCODE  =  "C"
           then
               go  to  I70-EX
           end-if.
           if  C-RETCODE  =  "E"
           then
               move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
               perform  T70-TESTO70    thru  T70-EX
               perform  W10-MSGERRORE thru  W10-EX
               go  to  I70-EX
           end-if.
           if  C-RETCODE  =  "D"
           then
               move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
               perform  T71-TESTO71    thru  T71-EX
               perform  W10-MSGERRORE thru  W10-EX
           end-if.
       I70-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       K10-KONTROLLO.
           move  spaces       to  W-FATTOCALCOLO.
      *------------------------------------------- Controllo dati STOP
           perform I70-DATISTRUTTURA     thru  I70-EX.
           if  W-ERRORE  =  "S"
           then
               go  to  K10-EX
           end-if.
      *------------------------------------------- Ristampe          *
           if  L-RICHIESTA  =  "R"
           then
               perform  K30-CHK-RISTAMPE thru  K30-EX
               if  W-ERRORE  =  "S"
               then
                   go  to  K10-EX
               end-if
               go  to  K10-SALTO1
           end-if.
      *------------------------------------------- Dati calcolo/pagamen
           perform  K20-CHK-DATICALCOLO  thru  K20-EX.
           if  W-ERRORE  =  "S"
           then
               go  to  K10-EX
           end-if.
      *------------------------------------------- Dati rec.analitici
           perform  K25-CHK-LANALITICO   thru  K25-EX.
           if  W-ERRORE  =  "S"
           then
               go  to  K10-EX
           end-if.
      *------------------------------------------- Memorizzo esecuzione
           perform  I60-BLOCCO           thru  I60-EX.
           if  W-ERRORE  =  "S"
           then
               go  to  K10-EX
           end-if.
       K10-SALTO1.
      *---------------------------------------- Controllo centraliz. *
           perform I13-CENTRA        thru  I13-EX.
      *    if  W-ERRORE  =  "S"
      *    then
      *        go  to  K10-EX
      *GG  end-if.
      *------------------------------------------- Lettura fuori ciclo
      *
            IF  L-RICHIESTA  NOT =  "R"
                PERFORM K25-DB2-DECL-CURS    THRU
                        K25-DB2-DECL-CURS-EX
            END-IF.
      *
           PERFORM E30-DB2-FETCH  THRU E30-DB2-FETCH-EX.
           IF SQLCODE NOT = 0
                STRING "READ    "
                     "LDSAPRD1  "
                      F-LANALITICO
                DELIMITED BY SIZE INTO VO-DSPFM034
                move  "96" to  OUT-STATUS
                move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
                move  "E"  to  L-RETCODE
           end-IF.
       K10-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       K20-CHK-DATICALCOLO.
           initialize  DCLTDSRPG00.
           move  L-PROCEDURA      to  H-PPROCEDURA .
           move  L-CODICE-STOP    to  H-PSTRUTTURA .
      *    move  L-PROGRESSIVO  to  H-PPROGRESSI.
           move  "N"              to  H-PBACKUP    .
      *
           PERFORM K20-DB2-SELECT THRU K20-DB2-SELECT-EX.
           IF SQLCODE NOT = 0
               move  "N"        to  W-FATTOCALCOLO
           ELSE
               move  "S"        to  W-FATTOCALCOLO
           end-IF.
      *-------------------------------------- Verifica
           if  W-FATTOCALCOLO  =  "S"
           then
               if  H-PFINEPAGAM                 =  "S"
               then
                   move  zeros       to  W8-AAAAMMGG
                                         D8-GGMMAAAA
                   move  H-PDATAELABO
                                     to  W8-AAAAMMGG
                     move  W8-GG     to  D8-GG
                     move  W8-MM     to  D8-MM
                     move  W8-AAAA   to  D8-AAAA
      *            move  D8-GGMMAAAA to
      *                                  S5D102  S5D202
               else
                   move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
                   perform  T73-TESTO73    thru  T73-EX
                   perform  W10-MSGERRORE thru  W10-EX
                   go  to  K20-EX
               end-if
               if  C-ELABINCORSO  =  "K"
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
                   perform  T76-TESTO76    thru  T76-EX
                   perform  W10-MSGERRORE thru  W10-EX
                   go  to  K20-EX
               end-if
               if  (H-PPROGRESSI =                 L-PROGRESSIVO)  and
                   (H-PPROGRESSI =                 C-PROGRESSIVO)
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
                   perform  T73-TESTO73    thru  T73-EX
                   perform  W10-MSGERRORE thru  W10-EX
                   go  to  K20-EX
               end-if
           else
               move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
               perform  T73-TESTO73    thru  T73-EX
               perform  W10-MSGERRORE thru  W10-EX
           end-if.
       K20-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       K25-CHK-LANALITICO.
           move  L-PROCEDURA      to  H-O0PROCEDURA.
           move  L-CODICE-STOP    to  H-O0DCOCENOPE.
           move  L-PROGRESSIVO    to  H-O0PROGRESSI.
           move  H-PDATAELABO
                              to  H-O0DATAELABO.
      *
           PERFORM K25-DB2-DECL-CURS    THRU  K25-DB2-DECL-CURS-EX.
           IF SQLCODE NOT = 0
               move  "N"        to  W-RECANALITICI
           ELSE
               move  "S"        to  W-RECANALITICI
           end-IF.
      *-------------------------------------- Verifica
           if  W-RECANALITICI  =  "S"
           then
               continue
           else
               move  "S"  to  W-ERRORE
               perform  T72-TESTO72    thru  T72-EX
               perform  W10-MSGERRORE thru  W10-EX
               go  to  K25-EX
           end-if.
       K25-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       K30-CHK-RISTAMPE.
           initialize  DCLTDSRPG00.
      *
      *-------------------------------------- Ultimo pagamento?      *
      *
           move  L-PROCEDURA    to  H-PPROCEDURA.
           move  L-CODICE-STOP  to  H-PSTRUTTURA.
           move  "N"            to  H-PBACKUP   .
           move  L-PROGRESSIVO  to  H-PPROGRESSI.
           move  L-DATAELABO    to  H-PDATAELABO
           PERFORM K30R-DB2-SELECT THRU K30R-DB2-SELECT-EX
           IF SQLCODE NOT = 0
               move  "N"        to  W-FATTOCALCOLO
           ELSE
               move  "S"        to  W-FATTOCALCOLO
           end-IF.
      *
      *-------------------------------------- Pagamento in storico?  *
      *
           if  W-FATTOCALCOLO  =  "N"
           then
               move  L-PROCEDURA    to  H-PPROCEDURA
               move  L-CODICE-STOP  to  H-PSTRUTTURA
               move  "S"            to  H-PBACKUP
               move  L-PROGRESSIVO  to  H-PPROGRESSI
               move  L-DATAELABO    to  H-PDATAELABO
               PERFORM K30-DB2-SELECT THRU K30-DB2-SELECT-EX
               IF SQLCODE NOT = 0
                   move  "N"        to  W-FATTOCALCOLO
                   move  "S"        to  W-ERRORE
                   perform  T73-TESTO73    thru  T73-EX
                   perform  W10-MSGERRORE thru  W10-EX
                   go  to  K30-EX
               ELSE
                   move  "S"        to  W-FATTOCALCOLO
               end-IF
           end-if.
      *
      *------------------------------------------- dati mappa        *
      *
           move  zeros       to  W8-AAAAMMGG
                                 D8-GGMMAAAA.
           move  H-PDATAELABO
                             to  W8-AAAAMMGG.
           move  W8-GG       to  D8-GG.
           move  W8-MM       to  D8-MM.
           move  W8-AAAA     to  D8-AAAA.
      *    move  D8-GGMMAAAA to
      *                          S5D102  S5D202.
      *
      *------------------------------------------- Dati rec.analitici*
      *
           perform  K25-CHK-LANALITICO
           thru     K25-EX.
       K30-EX.  exit.
      *
       K30R-DB2-SELECT.
      *
           MOVE  'K30R-DB2-SELECT' TO  WABNDB-LABEL.
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    H-PCOSEDE.
      *
           EXEC SQL
           SELECT
                H_PPROGRESSI,
                H_PDATAELABO,
                H_PCALCOLOAL,
                H_PCALCOLATI,
                H_PRECPAGATI,
                H_PFINEPAGAM,
                H_PZEROPAGAM,
                H_PIMPCONTAB,
                H_PIMPTELEMA,
                H_PCODTELEMA,
                H_PDATAEMISS,
                H_PMATRICOLA,
                H_PCODPAGA01,
                H_PIMPPAGA01,
                H_PCHEDOMAND,
                H_PCHEPRESTA,
                H_PCHENUMERA
           INTO
                :H-PPROGRESSI,
                :H-PDATAELABO,
                :H-PCALCOLOAL,
                :H-PCALCOLATI,
                :H-PRECPAGATI,
                :H-PFINEPAGAM,
                :H-PZEROPAGAM,
                :H-PIMPCONTAB,
                :H-PIMPTELEMA,
                :H-PCODTELEMA,
                :H-PDATAEMISS,
                :H-PMATRICOLA,
                :H-PCODPAGA01,
                :H-PIMPPAGA01,
                :H-PCHEDOMAND,
                :H-PCHEPRESTA,
                :H-PCHENUMERA
              FROM TDSRPG00
              WHERE
                     H_PPROCEDURA   =  :H-PPROCEDURA
                AND  H_PSTRUTTURA   =  :H-PSTRUTTURA
                AND  H_PPROGRESSI   =  :H-PPROGRESSI
                AND  H_PDATAELABO   =  :H-PDATAELABO
                AND  H_PCOSEDE      =  :H-PCOSEDE
                AND  H_PBACKUP      =  :H-PBACKUP
           END-EXEC.
           move  SQLCODE               to  F-LRIEPILOGO.
      *
           IF SQLCODE NOT = ZERO AND NOT = 100
               DISPLAY 'DCLTDSRPG00=' DCLTDSRPG00
               MOVE 'TDSRPG00'    TO  WABNDB-TABL
               MOVE 'SELECT'      TO  WABNDB-FUNC
               PERFORM ERRORE-SQL
           END-IF.
      *
       K30R-DB2-SELECT-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
      *-----------------------------------------------Testi msg
      *
       T04-TESTO04.
           move  spaces  to  M4A011  M4A012  M4A013  M4A014.
           move  "ATTENZIONE:  errore generico nella consultazione  "
           to    M4A011.
           move  "dei valori di sistema;                            "
           to    M4A012.
           move  "                        Il programma termina.     "
           to    M4A013.
           move  '96'               to  OUT-STATUS.
       T04-EX.  exit.
      *
       T05-TESTO05.
           move  spaces  to  M4A011  M4A012  M4A013  M4A014.
           move  "ATTENZIONE:  errore generico bloccante  nella     "
           to    M4A011.
           move  "richiesta di elaborazione.                        "
           to    M4A012.
           move  "                        Il programma termina.     "
           to    M4A013.
           move  '96'               to  OUT-STATUS.
       T05-EX.  exit.
      *
       T12-TESTO12.
           move  spaces  to  M4A011  M4A012  M4A013  M4A014.
           move  "     Attenzione: sono in atto altre elaborazioni  "
           to    M4A011.
           move  "sullo stesso archivio, incompatibili con la fase  "
           to    M4A012.
           move  "richiesta.                                        "
           to    M4A013.
           move  "                       Il programma termina.      "
           to    M4A014.
           move  '96'               to  OUT-STATUS.
       T12-EX.  exit.
      *
       T14-TESTO14.
           move  spaces  to  M4A011  M4A012  M4A013  M4A014.
           move  "     Attenzione: risulta già in uso l archivio di "
           to    M4A011.
           move  "ANALITICO  per il pagamento  della  indennità di  "
           to    M4A012.
           move  "disoccupazione ordinaria.                         "
           to    M4A013.
           move  "                       Il programma termina.      "
           to    M4A014.
           move  '96'               to  OUT-STATUS.
       T14-EX.  exit.
      *
       T70-TESTO70.
           move  spaces  to  M4A011  M4A012  M4A013  M4A014.
           move  "ATTENZIONE:  Si è verificato un errore non gestito"
           to    M4A011.
           move  "nella consultazione dei  dati della struttura e   "
           to    M4A012.
           move  "quindi non è possibile continuare l elaborazione. "
           to    M4A013.
           move  '96'               to  OUT-STATUS.
       T70-EX.  exit.
      *
       T71-TESTO71.
           move  spaces  to  M4A011  M4A012  M4A013  M4A014.
           move  "ATTENZIONE:  La  struttura  operativa  in uso  non"
           to    M4A011.
           move  "risulta  abilitata  alla  presenta  procedura  di "
           to    M4A012.
           move  "pagamento delle prestazioni: le relative funzioni "
           to    M4A013.
           move  "vengono inibite.                                  "
                to  M4A014.
           move  '96'               to  OUT-STATUS.
       T71-EX.  exit.
      *
       T72-TESTO72.
           move  spaces  to  M4A011  M4A012  M4A013  M4A014.
           move  "ATTENZIONE:  E  stata rilevata una contraddizione "
           to    M4A011.
           move  "tra le informazioni relative alla struttura ed i  "
           to    M4A012.
           move  "pagamenti delle prestazioni in corso. Contattare  "
           to    M4A013.
           move  "i  numeri di assistenza indicati nell aiuto (F1). "
           to    M4A014.
           move  '96'               to  OUT-STATUS.
       T72-EX.  exit.
      *
       T73-TESTO73.
           move  spaces  to  M4A011  M4A012  M4A013  M4A014.
           move  "ATTENZIONE:  Non sono presenti record di pagamento"
           to    M4A011.
           move  "relativi a codesta struttura, per i quali emettere"
           to    M4A012.
           move  "il documento richiesto.                           "
           to    M4A013.
           move  "                     Il programma termina.        "
           to    M4A014.
           move  '96'               to  OUT-STATUS.
       T73-EX.  exit.
      *
       T76-TESTO76.
           move  spaces  to  M4A011  M4A012  M4A013  M4A014.
           move  "Attenzione:  risulta avviata elaborazione da altra"
           to    M4A011.
           move  "unità sullo stesso archivio: il programma non può "
           to    M4A012.
           move  "continuare. Riprovare quando termina la fase in   "
           to    M4A013.
           move  "corso.                                            "
           to    M4A014.
           move  '96'               to  OUT-STATUS.
       T76-EX.  exit.
      *
       W10-MSGERRORE.
      *
           if  OUT-STATUS = '96' OR OUT-STATUS = '99'
           then
              move   VO-DSPFM034  to  OUT-MESSAGGIO
           end-if.
      *
       W10-EX.  exit.
      *--------------------------------------------------------*
       SCRIVI-TABINT1.
      *
090523     if  LMATRICOLA  =  "78360000"    and
               L-CODICE-SEDE  =  "0200"
           then
               display "NIK rdspd05,IMPDA      :   "  IMPDA
               display "NIK rdspd05,IMPAV      :   "  IMPAV
090523     end-if.
      *
           IF IMPDA > 0
               STRING ALFDA      DELIMITED BY SIZE
                      " "        DELIMITED BY SIZE
                      NUMDA      DELIMITED BY SIZE
      *               "/"        DELIMITED BY SIZE
      *               NUMDA(3:3) DELIMITED BY SIZE
                 INTO W-TR-CONTO
                 MOVE "D" TO W-TR-SEZIONE
                 MOVE IMPDA TO W-TR-IMPORTO
                 MOVE 1 TO IND-TR
                 PERFORM SCORRI-TABINT1 UNTIL IND-TR > 300
           END-IF.
           IF IMPAV > 0
               STRING ALFAV      DELIMITED BY SIZE
                      " "        DELIMITED BY SIZE
                      NUMAV      DELIMITED BY SIZE
                 INTO W-TR-CONTO
                 MOVE "A" TO W-TR-SEZIONE
                 MOVE IMPAV TO W-TR-IMPORTO
                 MOVE 1 TO IND-TR
                 PERFORM SCORRI-TABINT1 UNTIL IND-TR > 300
           END-IF.
      *
       SCRIVI-TABINT1-SPE.
           MOVE "GPA 24/042" TO W-TR-CONTO.
           MOVE "A" TO W-TR-SEZIONE
           MOVE RECSPE OF RIGASPE-O TO W-TR-IMPORTO
                                       WK-APP-RECSPE
           MOVE 1 TO IND-TR
           PERFORM SCORRI-TABINT1 UNTIL IND-TR > 300.
      *
       SCRIVI-TABINT1-IVA.
           MOVE "GPA 24/025" TO W-TR-CONTO.
           MOVE "A" TO W-TR-SEZIONE
           MOVE RECIVA OF RIGAIVA-O TO W-TR-IMPORTO
                                       WK-APP-RECIVA
           MOVE 1 TO IND-TR
           PERFORM SCORRI-TABINT1 UNTIL IND-TR > 300.
      *
       SCORRI-TABINT1.
GGA        IF  T-BCA-IMPORTO(IND-TR) = 0
      *    IF  T-BCA-CONTO(IND-TR) = SPACES
               MOVE W-TR-CONTO   TO T-BCA-CONTO(IND-TR)
               MOVE W-TR-SEZIONE TO T-BCA-SEZIONE(IND-TR)
               MOVE W-TR-IMPORTO TO T-BCA-IMPORTO(IND-TR)
               MOVE 301 TO IND-TR
           ELSE
               IF  W-TR-CONTO = T-BCA-CONTO(IND-TR)
               AND W-TR-SEZIONE = T-BCA-SEZIONE(IND-TR)
                   ADD W-TR-IMPORTO TO T-BCA-IMPORTO(IND-TR)
                   MOVE 301 TO IND-TR
               ELSE
                   ADD 1 TO IND-TR
               END-IF
           END-IF.
      *
090523     if  LMATRICOLA  =  "78360000"    and
               L-CODICE-SEDE  =  "0200"
           then
               display "NIK rdspd05, IND-TR  :   "  IND-TR
               display "NIK ,EL-TABINT1 :"  EL-TABINT1(IND-TR)
090523     end-if.
      *--------------------------------------------------------*
       CARICA-TABELLA-RECUPERI.
           MOVE 1 TO IND-R.
           MOVE 1 TO IND-REC.
           PERFORM UNTIL IND-R > 30
                      OR LRECCOREAL(IND-R) = SPACES
              MOVE 1 TO IND-REC
              PERFORM UNTIL IND-REC > 200
                 STRING LRECCORENU(IND-R)(1:2) DELIMITED BY SIZE
                        "/"                    DELIMITED BY SIZE
                        LRECCORENU(IND-R)(3:3) DELIMITED BY SIZE
                   INTO W-CONTO
                 IF  EL-ALF-REC-A(IND-REC) = SPACES
                    MOVE SPACES            TO EL-VOCE-REC(IND-REC)
                    MOVE LRECCOREAL(IND-R) TO EL-ALF-REC-A(IND-REC)
                    MOVE W-CONTO           TO EL-NUM-REC-A(IND-REC)
                    MOVE LRECIMUREE(IND-R) TO EL-IMP-REC-A(IND-REC)
                    MOVE 201 TO IND-REC
                 ELSE
                    IF  LRECCOREAL(IND-R) = EL-ALF-REC-A(IND-REC)
                    AND W-CONTO = EL-NUM-REC-A(IND-REC)
                       ADD LRECIMUREE(IND-R) TO EL-IMP-REC-A(IND-REC)
                       MOVE 201 TO IND-REC
                    ELSE
                       ADD 1 TO IND-REC
                    END-IF
                 END-IF
              END-PERFORM
              ADD 1 TO IND-R
           END-PERFORM.
       A10-DB2-SELECT.
      *
           MOVE  'A10-DB2-SELECT' TO  WABNDB-LABEL.
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    H-PCOSEDE.
      *
           EXEC SQL
           SELECT
                H_PPROGRESSI,
                H_PDATAELABO,
                H_PCALCOLOAL,
                H_PCALCOLATI,
                H_PRECPAGATI,
                H_PFINEPAGAM,
                H_PZEROPAGAM,
                H_PIMPCONTAB,
                H_PIMPTELEMA,
                H_PCODTELEMA,
                H_PDATAEMISS,
                H_PMATRICOLA,
                H_PCODPAGA01,
                H_PIMPPAGA01,
                H_PCHEDOMAND,
                H_PCHEPRESTA,
                H_PCHENUMERA
           INTO
                :H-PPROGRESSI,
                :H-PDATAELABO,
                :H-PCALCOLOAL,
                :H-PCALCOLATI,
                :H-PRECPAGATI,
                :H-PFINEPAGAM,
                :H-PZEROPAGAM,
                :H-PIMPCONTAB,
                :H-PIMPTELEMA,
                :H-PCODTELEMA,
                :H-PDATAEMISS,
                :H-PMATRICOLA,
                :H-PCODPAGA01,
                :H-PIMPPAGA01,
                :H-PCHEDOMAND,
                :H-PCHEPRESTA,
                :H-PCHENUMERA
              FROM TDSRPG00
              WHERE
                     H_PPROCEDURA   =  :H-PPROCEDURA
                AND  H_PSTRUTTURA   =  :H-PSTRUTTURA
                AND  H_PCOSEDE      =  :H-PCOSEDE
                AND  H_PBACKUP      =  :H-PBACKUP
           END-EXEC.
           move  SQLCODE               to  F-LRIEPILOGO.
      *
           IF SQLCODE NOT = ZERO AND NOT = 100
               DISPLAY 'DCLTDSRPG00=' DCLTDSRPG00
               MOVE 'TDSRPG00'    TO  WABNDB-TABL
               MOVE 'SELECT'      TO  WABNDB-FUNC
               PERFORM ERRORE-SQL
           END-IF.
      *
      *
       A10-DB2-SELECT-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       K20-DB2-SELECT.
      *
           MOVE  'K20-DB2-SELECT' TO  WABNDB-LABEL.
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    H-PCOSEDE.
      *
           EXEC SQL
           SELECT
                H_PPROGRESSI,
                H_PDATAELABO,
                H_PCALCOLOAL,
                H_PCALCOLATI,
                H_PRECPAGATI,
                H_PFINEPAGAM,
                H_PZEROPAGAM,
                H_PIMPCONTAB,
                H_PIMPTELEMA,
                H_PCODTELEMA,
                H_PDATAEMISS,
                H_PMATRICOLA,
                H_PCODPAGA01,
                H_PIMPPAGA01,
                H_PCHEDOMAND,
                H_PCHEPRESTA,
                H_PCHENUMERA
           INTO
                :H-PPROGRESSI,
                :H-PDATAELABO,
                :H-PCALCOLOAL,
                :H-PCALCOLATI,
                :H-PRECPAGATI,
                :H-PFINEPAGAM,
                :H-PZEROPAGAM,
                :H-PIMPCONTAB,
                :H-PIMPTELEMA,
                :H-PCODTELEMA,
                :H-PDATAEMISS,
                :H-PMATRICOLA,
                :H-PCODPAGA01,
                :H-PIMPPAGA01,
                :H-PCHEDOMAND,
                :H-PCHEPRESTA,
                :H-PCHENUMERA
              FROM TDSRPG00
              WHERE
                     H_PPROCEDURA   =  :H-PPROCEDURA
                AND  H_PSTRUTTURA   =  :H-PSTRUTTURA
                AND  H_PCOSEDE      =  :H-PCOSEDE
                AND  H_PBACKUP      =  :H-PBACKUP
           END-EXEC.
           move  SQLCODE               to  F-LRIEPILOGO.
      *
           IF SQLCODE NOT = ZERO AND NOT = 100
               DISPLAY 'DCLTDSRPG00=' DCLTDSRPG00
               MOVE 'TDSRPG00'    TO  WABNDB-TABL
               MOVE 'SELECT'      TO  WABNDB-FUNC
               PERFORM ERRORE-SQL
           END-IF.
      *
       K20-DB2-SELECT-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       K30-DB2-SELECT.
      *
           MOVE  'K30-DB2-SELECT' TO  WABNDB-LABEL.
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    H-PCOSEDE.
      *

                H_PPROGRESSI,
                H_PDATAELABO,

                H_PIMPPAGA01,

                H_PCHEPRESTA,
                H_PCHENUMERA
           INTO
                :H-PPROGRESSI,
                :H-PDATAELABO,
                :H-PCALCOLOAL,
                :H-PCALCOLATI,
                :H-PRECPAGATI,

                AND  H_PSTRUTTURA   =  :H-PSTRUTTURA
                AND  H_PPROGRESSI   =  :H-PPROGRESSI
                AND  H_PDATAELABO   =  :H-PDATAELABO
                AND  H_PCOSEDE      =  :H-PCOSEDE
                AND  H_PBACKUP      =  :H-PBACKUP
           END-EXEC.

      *

                AND  H_PSTRUTTURA     =  :H-PSTRUTTURA

              FROM        TDSVPIO0
              WHERE
                     H_O0COSEDE       =  :H-O0COSEDE
                AND  H_O0PROCEDURA    =  :H-O0PROCEDURA
                AND  H_O0DCOCENOPE    =  :H-O0DCOCENOPE
                AND  H_O0PROGRESSI    =  :H-O0PROGRESSI
           END-EXEC.
      *
           move  SQLCODE               to  F-LANALITICO.
      *
           IF SQLCODE NOT = ZERO AND NOT = 100
               DISPLAY 'DCLTDSVPIO0=' DCLTDSAPIO0
               MOVE 'TDSVPIO0'    TO  WABNDB-TABL
               MOVE 'SELECT '     TO  WABNDB-FUNC
               PERFORM ERRORE-SQL
           END-IF.

       E30-DB2-SELECT-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       E45-DB2-SELECT.
      *
           MOVE 'E45-DB2-SELECT'  TO WABNDB-LABEL.
      *
           EXEC SQL
           SELECT
                  H_CONDESCRI
                 INTO
                 :H-CONDESCRI
                 FROM TDSCONTB
                 WHERE
                          H_CONNUMERO      =  :H-CONNUMERO
           END-EXEC.
      *
           IF SQLCODE NOT = ZERO AND NOT = 100
               DISPLAY 'DCLTDSCONTB=' DCLTDSCONTB
               MOVE 'TDSCONTB'    TO  WABNDB-TABL
               MOVE 'SELECT '     TO  WABNDB-FUNC
               PERFORM ERRORE-SQL
           END-IF.
      *
       E45-DB2-SELECT-EX.
           EXIT.
270122****inizio mod
      ******************************************************************
       LEGGI-TAB.
      ******************************************************************

           MOVE 'LEGGI-TAB'       TO WABNDB-LABEL.

030222*inizio
      *    initialize h-wfrdetpvp.
      *
      *    EXEC SQL SELECT  H_WFRDETPVP
      *               INTO :H-WFRDETPVP
      *               FROM TDSWEBFV, TDSDATCO
      *              WHERE H_WFRNUMPROD  =  H_DCONUPRO
      *                AND H_WFRCODFIS   =  H_DCOCODFIS
      *                AND H_DCOCHIDOM   = :H-O0DCOCHIDOM
      *                AND H_DCOCODFIS   = :H-O0DCOCODFIS
      *     WITH UR
      *    END-EXEC.

           initialize h-sstalfl2.

           EXEC SQL SELECT  H_SSTALFL2
                      INTO :H-SSTALFL2
                      FROM TDSSUSST
                     WHERE H_SSTCHIDOM   = :H-O0DCOCHIDOM
            WITH UR
           END-EXEC.
030222*fine

           IF SQLCODE NOT = ZERO
               DISPLAY 'DCLTDSSUSST=' DCLTDSSUSST
               MOVE 'TDSSUSST'    TO  WABNDB-TABL
               MOVE 'SELECT '     TO  WABNDB-FUNC
               PERFORM ERRORE-SQL
           END-IF.

       EX-LEGGI-TAB.
           EXIT.
270122****fine mod
      *
       IMPOSTA-RPT.
      *
           MOVE FUNCTION CURRENT-DATE(1:14) TO WK-TIMESTAMP-DATA-ORA.
           MOVE WK-GG      TO  WW-DB2-GG.
           MOVE WK-MM      TO  WW-DB2-MM.
           MOVE WK-AA      TO  WW-DB2-AA.
           MOVE WK-H       TO  WW-DB2-HH.
           MOVE WK-M       TO  WW-DB2-T-MM.
           MOVE WK-S       TO  WW-DB2-SS.
           MOVE WK-DB2-DATA   TO TDSREPORT-DTA-PRE.
           MOVE WK-DB2-TIME   TO TDSREPORT-ORA-PRE.
           MOVE 8             TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RPT.
           MOVE 0             TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA.
           MOVE SPACES        TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT.
           MOVE L-CODICE-SEDE TO TDSREPORT-SEDE.
           MOVE L-CODICE-STOP TO TDSREPORT-CEOP.
           MOVE L-PROCEDURA   TO TDSREPORT-PROCEDURA.
           MOVE LMATRICOLA    TO TDSREPORT-MATRICOLA.
      *
           MOVE TDSREPORT-SEDE      TO WK-RPT-SEDE.
           MOVE TDSREPORT-CEOP      TO WK-RPT-CEOP.
           MOVE TDSREPORT-MATRICOLA TO WK-RPT-MATRICOLA.
           MOVE TDSREPORT-DTA-PRE   TO WK-RPT-DTA-PRE.
           MOVE TDSREPORT-ORA-PRE   TO WK-RPT-ORA-PRE.
      *
       EX-IMPOSTA-RPT.
           EXIT.
      *
      *----------------------------------------- COPY PER GESTIONE
      *
           EXEC SQL INCLUDE CDSABNDB END-EXEC.
